Description: Play your favorite songs straight from YouTube
Parameters:
	**play** [URL/Video Title] - Start playing/play a song from YouTube/SoundCloud
	**pause** - Pause the current song
	**volume** [0 - 100] - Changed the volume of the music. _Admin/DJ Overridable_
	**queue** [Page number] - View the Music queue and select which page
	**skip** - Vote to skip. Requires 40% of undefeaned users to skip

	**stop** - Stop the music
	**shuffle** - Shuffle the queue _Admin/DJ Only_
	**forceskip** - Force skip the song _Admin/DJ Only_
	**reset** - This completely resets the Music bot _Admin/DJ Only_
Example:
	_music play https://www.youtube.com/watch?v=dQw4w9WgXcQ_

02 Dec 2016 21:19:33 : The Wild Weebs, coding, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```def doubleSubstring(string : str):
    Matches = []
    while string is not "" and len(string) is not 1:
        found = False
        Start1 = 0
        End1 = 0
        Start2 = 1
        End2 = 1
        while string[Start1:End1+1] is not string[Start2:End2+1]:
            Start2 +=1
            End2 +=1
            print(string[Start1:End1+1] + ", " + string[Start2:End2+1])
            if(End2 > len(string) - 1):
                break
        while string[Start1:End1+1] == string[Start2:End2+1]:
            found = True
            End1 +=1
            End2 +=1
            print(string[Start1:End1+1] + " = " + string[Start2:End2+1])
        End1 -= 1
        End2 -= 1
        if End1 == 0:
            found = False
        print(string)
        if found:
            Matches.append(string[Start1:End1+1])
            string = string[:Start2] + string[End2+1:]
        else:
            string = string[1:]
    print(string)
    return Matches```

02 Dec 2016 21:20:19 : The Wild Weebs, coding, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```py
def doubleSubstring(string):
    Matches = []
    while string is not "" and len(string) is not 1:
        found = False
        Start1 = 0
        End1 = 0
        Start2 = 1
        End2 = 1
        while string[Start1:End1+1] is not string[Start2:End2+1]:
            Start2 +=1
            End2 +=1
            print(string[Start1:End1+1] + ", " + string[Start2:End2+1])
            if(End2 > len(string) - 1):
                break
        while string[Start1:End1+1] == string[Start2:End2+1]:
            found = True
            End1 +=1
            End2 +=1
            print(string[Start1:End1+1] + " = " + string[Start2:End2+1])
        End1 -= 1
        End2 -= 1
        if End1 == 0:
            found = False
        print(string)
        if found:
            Matches.append(string[Start1:End1+1])
            string = string[:Start2] + string[End2+1:]
        else:
            string = string[1:]
    print(string)
    return Matches```
